 ~ Louis Laborde: Hi everyone 👋

Welcome to this new group, which will be very useful during your semester in Würzburg for:

- Be informed of events organized for you by the Würzburg International Network (WIN) 
- Ask questions about life here (university, accommodation, etc.)
- Find people to do activities with (sports, visits, parties, etc.)

Basically, the aim is to keep a group where everyone can feel at ease, as was the case during the previous semester ✌️

To this end, a few basic rules: no sharing links, no ads to sell stuff, and other rules written in this group's descriptions.

👉 To invite other Erasmus / International students from Wü, use the link in the description of this group!
 ~ Louis Laborde: As a reminder, we (the WIN) are still on summer break for the time being, but as of September we'll be starting to organize events again so you can get to know each other and integrate into life here properly!

Once again, welcome to everyone, and don't hesitate to drop us a line if you have any questions 🫶

See you soon,
Your WIN Team.

 Stephan: Hello guys!
The Würzburg International Network (WIN) is a group of volunteers organizing events and free time activities for exchange students to make it easier for you to connect, create memories, and have a good time. Usually we meet every other week in order to plan upcoming activities. We are always open for new members and supporters no matter where you come from and what you study. The only necessary characteristic is reliability. Our next meeting is today at 7 pm. If you are interested in joining, please let me know. As a group of volunteers there are no strings attached and every member puts as much time and effort in as they want.
So come and check us out and become part of the WIN family. 👬🥳

 ~ Kimiya: Hi, does anyone know if you have to book the train from Frankfurt airport to Würzburg in advance? or can you buy on the day? I’m worries about booking and then my plane being delayed
 ~ Oliver: the earlier you book, the cheaper the price will be. It is always possible to just book it a few minutes prior to departure, but the price will be much higher. It is also possible to just book the connection, then it doesnt matter if you get exactly that train, or the next one going the same route
 ~ Alex: Take 49 Euro Ticket and travel by any regional train
 ~ Alex: Then you do not need to book the specific train
 ~ Alex: But the travel will be longer
‎ ~ Oliver: ‎immagine omessa
 ~ Alex: you can usually book on the day I have always done so and never had a problem, also its more likely the train is late 😅
 ~ Millie: Mine was like €34 and I booked it on the day x
 ~ Kimiya: I can only find ICE trains between Frankfurt and Würzburg? Where can I find regional trains?
 ~ Kimiya: Oh really that’s not too bad! Because if I buy a flexible ticket it will be €45!
 ~ Anurag Parida: If you're travelling for the first time, I highly suggest going old school and buying a ticket from the counter at the bahnhof in person, and only taking an ICE. It'll be more expensive, but you don't need to worry about timings as ICEs are very punctual, no delays, no changeovers (to würzburg), and wifi onboard in case you don't have a German sim yet
 ~ Anurag Parida: You'll have luggage, which is difficult to navigate in a filled RE/RB. ICEs are usually empty or barely filled
 ~ IgV: I think that for some journeys that are usually very common and short, the price is no that different when you buy in advance or at the moment
 ~ IgV: I bought my ticket in the db navigator app when I already had my luggage, so I was sure that I would make the train, and did not cost me more
 ~ Anurag Parida: True, but it really depends. My ticket from FRA to Schweinfurt was 38 in advance, 54 when I bought it at the counter. It's octoberfest season soon too.
 ~ Alex: If you use DB Navigator you need to check options ans set only regional trains. It usually will be two trains: airport - Nürnberg Main Station, Nürnberg Main Station - Würzburg
 ~ IgV: But in my case it was first Frankfurt-Heidelberg so I don't know if the prices are similar to Frankfurt-Würzburt
 ~ Abhinav: I bought my ticket from FRK to Wü yesterday for Oct 5th and the basic ticket cost me 18€ for the ICE
 ~ Alex: Also highly agreed, DB can be so fucked up, trains are late or event stops are cancelled in some stations

 ~ Alex: 🏖️ *FREIBAD TAG*

This Sunday, from 13:00–17:00, we are going to the biggest outdoor swimming pool in Würzburg: Dallenbergbad! 
They have big pools and grass areas to enjoy the day, as well as outdoor activities (Volleyball, etc.), different slides, and jump towers.

Since the weather should be excellent we can all spend there an amazing day. The entrance for the entire day is only 3,50€ (with your student ID). Make sure to bring suncream, drinks, food, towels, games, and everything you need there. We are looking forward to have a great time with you and meet each other at 13:00 at the entrance!

📍 Dallenbergbad (König-Heinrich-Straße 52)
⏰ Sunday 10.09. (meeting 13:00)
💰 3,50€ (student's entry fee)

See you there,
Your WIN Team

 Stephan: No. It depends on several parameters. And it depends on what kind of tax you mean. You'll be taxed for healthcare, retirement, unemployment etc. but probably there wont be an income tax.
 ~ Alex: Lets start from the scratch. 
- In Germany Yearly you can each 10.908 Euros without paying tax. Everything that is bigger will be taxed. 
- Second of all anyway you will pay around 9% for pension tax
 ~ Alex: *earn
 ~ Bengisu Kaya: Thank you
 ~ Alex: Third important: students working hours in sum should not be higher than full-time worker for half a year(so we can say that students can work only half a year full time)
 Stephan: + tax for health care, unemployment, elderly care - In total about 20% social tax independent of income tax.
 Stephan: Oh well, I just remembered that social tax is lower as a student.
 ~ Alex: So if you work in a big company and the company offers it: ask your managers to pay for your:
-tickets
-car in leasing
-invest in stocks 
from your salary before the taxes are applied. But I am not sure they will do it for working students.
 Stephan: If you work as a student you have two options: Be employed as a student (Werkstudent) - pay less social tax, take care of health care yourself. Or be employed as an employee (Arbeitnehmer) - more social tax but health care is included.

 ~ Saleh: Take Dogs and Other Pets with You
Do you want to bring your dog and other pets on your journey? Simply book online or through the app here.
Note: Dogs that do not travel in a transport box must be leashed and wear a muzzle.

Your Benefits
For small dogs and other small pets (up to the size of a house cat), you don't need a ticket if the animals are carried in a suitable transport container.
For larger dogs, you need a separate ticket. You only pay half the fare.
Dogs that do not travel in a transport box must be leashed and wear a muzzle.
Guide dogs for the blind and marked assistance dogs always travel free of charge and do not need to wear a muzzle on the train.
 ~ Saleh: This is from DB website
 ~ Saleh: You need to book a ticket for any unboxed Dog

Are you interested in learning new languages and intercultural exchanges? Würzburg International Meetup organises a language exchange event every Wednesday. The event is always held at Capri Blaue Grotto, Elefantengasse 1, 97070 Würzburg. It's the oldest pizzeria in Germany and offers a wide variety of Italian and Spanish food on the plate.  ~ Edward: What’s the best wifi to get for student who will only be here for a semester?
 ~ Anthony: Deutschlandticket special offer for Würzburg students!

Starting 1 October 2023, you can travel by local trains & buses all across Germany with the Deutschlandticket for a special price of only €15 per month for Würzburg students! This is optional on top of the €14 per month you are required to pay for the semester ticket within the VVM service area (Würzburg & the surrounding areas)

*If you already have an existing regular Deutschlandticket subscription, you must unsubscribe it first before the 10th of the final month you're using it, as the ticket type cannot be automatically changed.*

You can only buy this ticket online from either the *WVV app* using evidence of an immatriculation certificate, or the *Deutschlandticket Mainfranken website* using login with your online credentials & have your ticket saved in Google or Apple Wallet on your device. It is NOT obtainable from ticket machines, bus drivers, or other operators.

How to buy from WVV:
1. Download the "WVV mobil" app or open the "WVV Webshop" on your browser.
2. Create an account, then input your payment method (currently accepts auto debit from either a European/SEPA bank account, credit card, or Paypal).
3. Once you are logged in, go to the "Deutschlandticket" menu, choose the "Deutschlandticket Studium" that costs €15 per month. On the next page, choose the month of when you want to start the subscription, then click the word "click here". It will lead you to another page where you can upload your *immatriculation certificate* from one of the Würzburg colleges: Uni Würzburg, THWS, Hochschule für Musik.
4. You will receive an email from WVV within 3 working days regarding your eligibility. The ticket can then finally be purchased from the same page.
5. Your ticket can then at anytime be accessed through the "Pinboard" menu in the app.

The ticket allows you to take all local public transports within Germany and a few steps beyond the borders. It is not valid on first class, the ICE fast trains & private operators (e.g. Flixbus/Flixtrain). The ticket is NOT transferable (i.e. other people cannot use your ticket, as you may be required to show an ID that has the same name as on the ticket.) and you can only have one ticket per device.

6. Regardless of the date of purchase, the ticket is valid for the whole calendar month stated until 3AM on the 1st day of the following month.
7. The ticket renews automatically for the following month. If you wish to stop using it, don't forget to click "unsubscribe now" at the bottom of the ticket page by the 10th of the final month you will be using it.
8. If you are staying for more than one semester, you will be required to upload a new immatriculation certificate for the following semester(s), when prompted to do so.

Have a happy & safe travels around Germany!

Disclaimer: Information here may change at anytime without notice. And of course, this post is not sponsored, but solely extracted based on the information available in German.

 ~ Anthony: *A quick reminder...if you want to travel around Germany using the Deutschlandticket for a reduced rate of €15/month and start using it from 1 October (this Sunday), you need to buy it using the WVV mobil app & provide your student immatriculation & be verified by then. You can already buy the tickets now if you had been verified. Here's how to buy it:*

*Deutschlandticket special offer for Würzburg students!*

Starting 1 October 2023, you can travel by local trains & buses all across Germany with the Deutschlandticket for a special price of only €15 per month for Würzburg students! This is optional on top of the €14 per month you are required to pay for the semester ticket within the VVM service area (Würzburg & the surrounding areas)

*If you already have an existing normal rate Deutschlandticket subscription, you must unsubscribe it first before the 10th of the final month you're using it, as the ticket type cannot be automatically changed and so that you will not be double charged for the following month.*

You can only buy this ticket online, either from the *WVV mobil app* using evidence of an immatriculation certificate, or the *Deutschlandticket Mainfranken website* using login with your online credentials & then have your ticket saved in Google or Apple Wallet on your device. It is NOT available in ticket machines or counters, bus drivers, or other operators.

How to buy from WVV mobil:
1. Download the *WVV mobil* app or open the "WVV Webshop" (ticketswvv.de) on your browser.
2. Create an account, then input your payment method (currently accepts auto debit from either a European/SEPA bank account, a credit card, or Paypal).
3. Once you are logged in, go to the "Deutschlandticket" menu, choose the "Deutschlandticket Studium" that costs €15 per month. On the next page, choose the month of when you want to start the subscription, then click the word "click here". It will lead you to another page where you can upload your *immatriculation certificate* from one of the Würzburg colleges: Uni Würzburg, THWS, Hochschule für Musik.
4. You will receive an email from WVV within 3 working days regarding your eligibility. The ticket can then finally be purchased from the same page.
5. Your ticket can then at anytime be accessed through the "Pinboard" menu in the app.

The ticket allows you to take all local public transports within Germany and a few steps beyond the borders. It is NOT valid on the ICE fast trains & private operators (e.g. Flixbus/Flixtrain). The ticket is NOT transferable (i.e. other people cannot use your ticket, as you may be required to show an ID that has the same name as on the ticket.) and you can only have one ticket per device.

6. Regardless of the date of purchase (you can buy from 3 months before the validity begins), the ticket is valid for the whole calendar month as stated, from midnight on the first day until 3AM on the 1st day of the following month.
7. The ticket renews automatically for the following month. If you wish to stop using it, don't forget to click "unsubscribe now" at the bottom of the ticket page by the 10th of the final month you will be using it.
8. If you are staying for more than one semester, you will need to upload a new immatriculation certificate for the following semester(s), when prompted to do so.

Have a happy & safe travels around Germany!

 ~ Der Max™️: *All seats are taken!*
Don't worry if you couldn't sign up this time. This will be one of our regular events happening every month!

*Doors open at 18:30* and we start the show at 19:00.
Please remember to *bring cash* with you. You can buy drinks at the bar at fair student prices. Please note that the bartenders in the Kellerperle are paid by tip (usually about 10% in Germany) and that *you cannot come to the bar with your own drinks*. Some snacks may also be available.

Please also remember to keep to the maximum number of participants of 6 per team! We do not allow any team to have more than 6 participants, otherwise you will have an unfair advantage over the other teams. Furthermore, we ask you to put your mobile phone away during the trivia rounds. So there won't be any cheating allegations. 😉

We are looking forward to have a wonderful and fun evening with you! 
See you later, your WIN Trivia Team🫶

 ~ Quang Minh: ICE for the most convinience :D, RE you will have to switch train a lot
 ~ IgV: The intermediate plan would be to get an ICE but only for the cheapest part of the trip that you can find, so you short the 10 hrs regional trip. If you are going to stay in Germany for almoast a year or more, you can also get the bahncard 25 thar it is now in offer, and you get a 25% discount on the ICE
 ~ IgV: Maybe just see which regional train(s) would be the longest one(s) and try to find an alternative with ICE that should be cheaper that the single ICE to Hamburg (maybe)
 ~ IgV: but basically just play with DB navigator to see what fits you best

 ~ Der Max™️: 🍷*WINE TOUR REMINDER*

Hello everyone who signed up for our wine walk. 😊

Meeting point is at 15:15 and 17:15 in front of the Hubland Library (https://maps.app.goo.gl/Mg9EgZFkL44L5KaJA). Please be on time, because we will start heading to the vineyards.
During the tour you will get to taste a selection of wines from the region. *Please refrain from bringing your own wine* (or beer for that matter). After the tour you can head to Randersacker and go to a wine bar or take the bus to head back to Würzburg. 

We hope you have a great time and learn something about wine and wine making. 😊🍷

(This also applies to the Saturday tours)

See you later,
Your WIN Team 🫶
